"diagnoses of superficial injury of head\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of superficial injury of head. superficial injury of head is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code s00. icd-10 also has the following superficial injury of head children in its four-character category: s00.0 (superficial injury of scalp ); s00.1 (contusion of eyelid and periocular area ); s00.2 (other superficial injuries of eyelid and periocular area ); s00.3 (superficial injury of nose ); s00.4 (superficial injury of ear ); s00.5 (superficial injury of lip and oral cavity ); s00.7 (multiple superficial injuries of head ); s00.8 (superficial injury of other parts of head ); s00.9 (superficial injury of head, part unspecified ). . "

"diagnoses of intracranial injury\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of intracranial injury. intracranial injury is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code s06. icd-10 also has the following intracranial injury children in its four-character category: s06.0 (concussion ); s06.1 (traumatic cerebral oedema ); s06.2 (diffuse brain injury ); s06.3 (focal brain injury ); s06.4 (epidural haemorrhage ); s06.5 (traumatic subdural haemorrhage ); s06.6 (traumatic subarachnoid haemorrhage ); s06.7 (intracranial injury with prolonged coma ); s06.8 (other intracranial injuries ); s06.9 (intracranial injury, unspecified ). . "diagnoses of other injuries of head\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of other and unspecified injuries of head. other and unspecified injuries of head is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code s09. icd-10 also has the following other and unspecified injuries of head children in its four-character category: s09.0 (injury of blood vessels of head, not elsewhere classified ); s09.1 (injury of muscle and tendon of head ); s09.2 (traumatic rupture of ear drum ); s09.7 (multiple injuries of head ); s09.8 (other specified injuries of head ); s09.9 (unspecified injury of head ); s10.0 (contusion of throat ); s10.1 (other and unspecified superficial injuries of throat ); s10.7 (multiple superficial injuries of neck ); s10.8 (superficial injury of other parts of neck ); s10.9 (superficial injury of neck, part unspecified ). . "

"diagnoses of dislocation, sprain and strain of joints and ligaments at neck level\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of dislocation, sprain and strain of joints and ligaments at neck level. dislocation, sprain and strain of joints and ligaments at neck level is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code s13. icd-10 also has the following dislocation, sprain and strain of joints and ligaments at neck level children in its four-character category: s13.0 (traumatic rupture of cervical intervertebral disc ); s13.1 (dislocation of cervical vertebra ); s13.2 (dislocation of other and unspecified parts of neck ); s13.3 (multiple dislocations of neck ); s13.4 (sprain and strain of cervical spine ); s13.5 (sprain and strain of thyroid region ); s13.6 (sprain and strain of joints and ligaments of other and unspecified parts of neck ). . "
